", "date_post": "Mar 02, 2019", "link_review": "https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2664077471?book_show_action=true&from_review_page=1", "comment": ["People love it because it's realistic. A good novel doesn't always have to have perfect characters. If you want perfect and likeable characters that much, you should read \"The Notebook\". Yes, Ngạn sounds like a loser, Hà Lan must be a utilitarian girl, Dũng is an f-boy. But that's why this story could have touched so many people- because it's realistic and it's relatable. We don't need to be gods to love, to hate, to have meaningful memories and bitter experiences. Ngạn, as I said- is just a below-average guy, but his loyal with Ha Lan is a symbol for a type of love that so many people on earth have experienced: the innocent, no self-interest emotions toward your crush, your first love. Sometimes this type of love is harmful to both of the parties, but it's love regardless and that's why Ngạn's emotions toward Hà Lan in this novel should be seen with empathy even they are not sensible at all. Hà Lan can be observed as a typical beautiful girl who changes her environment from rural to urban. Her life can turn in two directions - either to become independent and to be happy, or it can also be very painful. Nguyễn Nhật Ánh made her make a choice and we should not criticise it, but to learn from her decision's consequences. Furthermore- About Dũng, I don't think he's that bad. Yeah, he's pretty bad, but in this novel, he represents the guys who are young and have nothing to worry about life and/or financial problems. Guys like that can be carefree, heartless or to be seen by some people as cruel but it's a fact of life and there is little thing we can do about it other than protecting and improving ourselves. And lastly, Trà Long- a cute girl with all the good traits, but turns out to be just a copy or someone else's replacement. It's bitter and it's hard to accept, but again it's realistic. Trust me, if you dive deep enough into love, someday you may find yourself- or your partner just to be a replacement for a ghost of the past. But I hope that you all won't have to live a whole life in that role, and that's what Nguyễn Nhật Ánh are trying to say with us, by using Ngạn and Trà Long. So, did you see? \"Mắt biếc\" is not a perfect love story, not even a good story. But it's a great novel about the love and the life of young Vietnamese people in the 60s (or 70s). The emotions in the novel are real, and I think that not only you and me, or people nowaday but also people in the future can feel related to it. Because it's love, and love is eternal."]}, {"user_id": 9622995, "name_user": "Victoria", "rate": 1, "review_content": "OK THIS IS THE WORST BOOK I'VE EVER READ WOMEN'S RIGHTS-sadboy romanticizes childhood love and pines after her for the rest of his life-raises her daughter from another dude-FALLS IN LOVE WITH DAUGHTER????-leaves bc that's fucked up -other themes of like modern city life vs. tradition and love for your rural hometown, but also like dude is so uselessly sad and creepy im writing the synopsis bc no one else is going to read this book but damn! women's rights ", "date_post": "Jul 05, 2020", "link_review": "https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3415156446?book_show_action=true&from_review_page=1", "comment": ["i'm laughing at this"]}, {"user_id": 71737494, "name_user": "Hoàng  Thu Thuỷ", "rate": 3, "review_content": "I am not a fan of NNA.
